RTL COURSE SYLLABUS in CCC298 SYSTEMATIC REVIEW AND RESEARCH SEMINAR IN ICT 
 
MSU-IIT 
Vision 
A research university committed to the 
holistic development of the individual and 
society. 
 
Mission 
To provide quality education for the 
sustainable development of the nation 
and the global community. 
 
COLLEGE OF COMPUTER 
STUDIES 
Vision 
A Center of Excellence in Information 
and Communication Technology manned 
by motivated and highly competent 
workforce who adheres to Institute 
policies; equipped with state- of-the-art 
infrastructure; founded on relevant 
instruction, strong culture of Research & 
Extension and enhanced resource-
generating programs producing highly 
competitive graduates imbued with 
professional values. 
 
Mission 
Transform the deserving sector of the 
society into highly competitive graduates 
who will respond to the needs of the Local 
and International industries for ICT 
professionals. 
 Course No./Title:  CCC298 SYSTEMATIC REVIEW AND RESEARCH SEMINAR IN ICT 
Course Credit:  3 units 
Duration: 18 weeks (Semester Year: _______) 
Delivery Mode:  Asynchronous (remotely supervised) with a few synchronous sessions 
Level: Advanced / Masters 
Course Description: A very dynamic and fast changing field of study, Information Systems being under the 
overarching computing discipline is constantly faced with updates that may need thorough 
discussion in either depth of breadth. This course will discuss speci al topics in information and 
communications technology (ICT) and will cover research trends and professional updates in 
the ICT profession that can be candidate research topics. In the midst of rapid global change 
that poses new opportunities to contribute development to different sectors of the society using 
ICT, this course aims to systematically analyze and identify these research opportunities. 
Students in this course will be required to conduct a structured review of related literature on a 
certain special topic in ICT as a preparation for  their thesis proposal. After the development of 
the structured review, students will be able to synthesize the research gaps and develop a 
conceptual framework for a proposed research. This course will train the students to choose a 
particular special research topic in ICT which is relevant to the local context of concern and 
develop a written report and present the analysis of methodologies, gaps, limitations and 
opportunities for possible ICT research. 
 
Part of the course is the Research Seminar, a forum to foster a research culture in the 
department and discuss the theoretical and practical issues of conducting research and 
completing a graduate degree in Information Systems, Information Technology, Computer 
Applications and Computer Science. As such, all College of Computer Studies graduate 
students are welcome and encouraged to attend the scheduled lectures, presentations, and

colloquium (a graduation requirement for all Masters students). For that purpose, the  goal is to 
learn the practical skills of giving a presentation and prepare for writing a research proposal.  
Learning Culminating 
Outcome: 
By the end of this course, the students should be able to come up with a report of literature analysis on a 
specialresearch topic in ICT. This course will require students to develop a written and orally presented 
structured review of related literature on a special ICT as well as a proposed conceptual framework which 
is relevant to a local context. By the end of this course, the students can articulate their research topic that 
can be further developed towards proposing the topic for their graduate thesis. 
Prerequisite: None 
Co-requisite: None 
Evaluation Criteria: Passing the course requires a passing grade on the written and oral presentation review of related 
literature

7 Present the research topic in a seminar setting  √ 
 
 
Course Outcomes: 
At the end of the term, students would be able to:  
a) Describe the possibility of research in a special topic of ICT related research. 
b) Review a survey of literature survey on a particular special topic. Develop an analysis on the gaps and research opportunities on a special 
topic in ICT related research. 
c) Demonstrate planning and organization of research work that meets the required/ timeline of the subject (thesis preparation) by executing 
the tasks to complete the needed components of the subject (thesis /preparation) 
d) Communicate the outcome of the research being undertaken through rigorous writing and present the research topic in a seminar setting

Classroom Polices: 
1. Observe excellent performance on the following: 
a) Honesty and Integrity; Punctuality/Attendance; Use class time appropriately; Remain in your seat until dismissed by your teacher. 
b) Use technology (i.e., Anycast, Bluetooth, WiFi, etc.) appropriately;  
c) Put cell phones and other noise makers on silent mode or turn them off. If you need to take a call, for some urgent or emergency reason, then 
please let the instructor know before class and then answer the call outside of the classroom. 
d) Follow obediently the computer laboratory policies implemented by the department. 
2. Respect the rights, opinions, ideas, and property of others: 
a) Be courteous.   
b) Raise hand before speaking.  
c) Perform class activities without interrupting/disturbing anyone.   
d) Use laboratory equipment properly to avoid accident, and ensure safety of others. 
3. Take active participation on class discussion, laboratory activities and department/college extracurricular activities 
4. Contribute to discussions by sharing new ideas, innovations and relevant researches 
5. Refrain/avoid inappropriate comments. 
6. Equality in the use of the laboratory facilities irrespective of gender. 
7. Observe 5S +1, (Sort, Set in order, Shine, Standardize, Sustain, and Safety). 
8. Stewards of environment thru the conduct of research related activities that protects the environment 
9. Involvement in the promotion on Green Technolog
